English

we shall proceed briefly to remove certain misconceptions
which arise from the relationship of spouse
that is expressed in the word ┼Ъr─лmat (having Lakс╣гm─л )
as existing between ┼Ъr─л and the Supreme Ruler
who has consecrated Himself for the sacrifice or yajna of saving all.

рдХреЗрдЪрд┐рджреН рджреНрд╡рдпреЗ рдкреВрд░реНрд╡рдЦрдгреНрдбреЗ рд╢реНрд░реАрдордЪреН-рдЫрдмреНрдж рдЙрдкрд▓рдХреНрд╖рдгрдкрд░ рдЗрддрд┐,

English

There are some who hold that,
in the former part of the Dvaya,
the word ┼Ъr─лmat is an Upalakс╣гaс╣Зa
( an accidental sign by which the thing is distinguished
and not a permanent attribute (or vi┼Ыeс╣гaс╣Зa)),
whereas in the latter part, the same word means a permanent attribute of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa .

(In “That is Devadatta’s field where the crane was sitting before”,
the crane is an Upalakс╣гaс╣Зa or accidental feature to identify the field with.
It is not a permanent attribute or vi┼Ыeс╣гaс╣Зa of the field.)

(If this were true, it would follow that the words
‘I seek as my refuge’ / ┼Ыaraс╣Зam prapadye
would apply only to N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa
and not to ┼Ъr─л or Lakс╣гm─л
who, in that part, according to them,
is not meant to be taken as an inseparable attribute
but as only an accidental mark to distinguish N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa.

Since in the latter part, Sr─лmat is, according to them, an inseparable attribute (vi┼Ыeс╣гana),
it would follow that the dative and the namah would apply to the attribute and the substantive, viz. Sr─л and Bhagav─Бn.
(It would then mean that
Lakс╣гm─л is not to be sought as the up─Бya
but that adoration and service are due to her as well as to her spouse, N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa ).

Espa├▒ol

Hay algunos que sostienen eso,
en la primera parte del dvaya,
La palabra ┼Ыr─лmat es un upalakс╣гaс╣Зa
(un signo accidental por el cual se distingue la cosa
y no un atributo permanente (o vi┼Ыeс╣гaс╣Зa)),
Mientras que en la ├║ltima parte,
la misma palabra significa un atributo permanente de N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa.

(En “Ese es el campo de Devadatta donde la gr├║a estaba sentada antes”,
La gr├║a es una caracter├нstica upalakс╣гaс╣Зa o accidental para identificar el campo.
No es un atributo permanente o vi┼Ыeс╣гaс╣Зa del campo).

(Si esto fuera cierto, seguir├нa que las palabras
‘Busco como mi refugio’ / ┼Ъaraс╣Зam Prapadye
se aplicar├нa solo a N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa
y no a ┼Ъr─л o Lakс╣гm─л
quien, en esa parte, seg├║n ellos,
no est├б destinado a ser tomado como un atributo inseparable
pero como solo una marca accidental para distinguir n─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa.

Dado que en la ├║ltima parte, Sr─лmat es, seg├║n ellos, un atributo inseparable (vi┼Ыeс╣гana),
Seguir├нa que el dativo y el namah se aplicar├нan al atributo y al sustantivo, a saber Sr─л y Bhagav─Бn.
(Entonces significar├нa que
Lakс╣гm─л no debe ser buscado como el up─Бya
pero esa adoraci├│n y servicio se deben a ella y a su c├│nyuge, N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa).

In this (wrong) view,
when the same word ┼Ъr─лmat is found in both the parts (of Dvaya)
and when there is no objection to interpreting it in the same way,
in both the places,

рдЗрддреНрдпреН-рдЖрджрд┐рд╖реБ рдкреНрд░рд╕рд┐рджреНрдзрд╕реНрдп рдХреВрдЯрд╕реНрде-рд╕рдВрдкреНрд░рджрд╛рдпрд╕реНрдп рд╡рд┐рд░реБрджреНрдзрддрдпрд╛ рдХреНрд░рд┐рдпрдорд╛рдгреЛрд╜рдпрдВ рд╡рд┐рднрд╛рдЧреЛ рд╜рдиреБрдкрдкрдиреНрдирдГ ред

English

the adoption of an interpretation
which is at variance with the well-known view of the ancient ─Бc─Бryas
and with the tradition connected with Nammalvar, the chief of all prapannas
and which would give two different interpretations to the same word in the same sentence
has no justification.
For in the following ┼Ыloka it is said :-

“O Lakс╣гm─л , with a face delightful like the moon!
When (we) try to study Thee as distinct from Bhagav─Бn,
(we feel) that His svar┼лpa or essential nature and His being the Ruler over all
are the consequence of the greatness, which is His,
by His being ever with Thee.
Thou art, therefore, the part (or attribute) by which Bhagav─Бn is understood
as being of such and such a character.
Since Thou and Bhagav─Бn are thus (inseparably) united,
the Veda does not speak of Thee separately”.

Espa├▒ol

la adopci├│n de una interpretaci├│n
que est├б en desacuerdo con la conocida visi├│n de los antiguos ─Бc─Бryas
y con la tradici├│n conectada con Nammalvar, el jefe de todas las Prapannas
y que dar├нan dos interpretaciones diferentes a la misma palabra en la misma oraci├│n
no tiene justificaci├│n.
Porque en el siguiente ┼Ъloka se dice:-

“┬бOh Lakс╣гm─л, con una cara encantadora como la luna!
Cuando (nosotros) tratamos de estudiarte como distinto de Bhagav─Бn,
(sentimos) que su svar┼лpa o naturaleza esencial y su ser el gobernante sobre todo
son la consecuencia de la grandeza, que es suya,
Por su ser siempre contigo.
T├║ eres, por lo tanto, la parte (o atributo) por la cual se entiende Bhagav─Бn
como ser de tal y tal personaje.
Dado que t├║ y Bhagav─Бn est├бn, por lo tanto, (inseparablemente) unidos,
El Veda no habla de ti por separado”.

English

If it is now asked:

“In that case what is the objection to taking the word ┼Ъr─лmat
as only an accidentally associated mark (Upalakс╣гaс╣Зa)
by which Bhagav─Бn is distinguished
in both the parts of the Dvaya”,

the answer is as follows:–

Certain qualities, certain forms ( vigrahas) and certain activities are necessary for I┼Ыvara being the up─Бya.
Likewise certain other qualities, certain other forms and certain activities are ever associated with I┼Ыvara as the object of attainment.
These necessary ( things ), also, would be at variance with I┼Ыvara being the only up─Бya and the only object of attainment respectively.
So they, too, would have to be considered as accidental features and not inseparable attributes,
but this would be against the view of these critics
who hold that I┼Ыvara is the Protector or Saviour only in virtue of (such attributes as) His omnipotence and His compassion.
So they cannot concede that these qualities are only accidental features (Upalakс╣гaс╣Зa).

por el cual se distingue bhagav─Бn

La respuesta es la siguiente:-

Ciertas cualidades, ciertas formas (Vigrahas) y ciertas actividades son necesarias para que I┼Ыvara sea el up─Бya.
Del mismo modo, ciertas otras cualidades, ciertas otras formas y ciertas actividades est├бn asociadas con I┼Ыvara como objeto de logro.
Estas (cosas) necesarias, tambi├йn, estar├нan en desacuerdo con que I┼Ыvara sea el ├║nico up─Бya y el ├║nico objeto de logro respectivamente.

Pero esto estar├нa en contra de la opini├│n de estos cr├нticos
quienes sostienen que I┼Ыvara es el protector o salvador solo en virtud de (tales atributos como) su omnipotencia y su compasi├│n.
Por lo tanto, no pueden admitir que estas cualidades son solo caracter├нsticas accidentales (upalakс╣гaс╣Зa).

both in the first part of the Dvaya and in the second part of the Dvaya.
(i.e.) (She, too, is useful for the respective purposes ).

English

The great sage Par─Б┼Ыara
who received the knowledge concerning the truth about the Supreme Deity
from boons granted to him by Vasiс╣гс╣нa and Pulastya
has stated

“Thou art, O Goddess, the knowledge concerning the soul,
the giver of mokс╣гa ,
the object of attainment .”

(The ┼Ыloka says:

Thou art the knowledge concerning the self or atma vidy─Б,

Lakс╣гm─л is in apposition with atma vidy─Б.
The meaning is that atma vidy─Б is one of her vibh┼лtis or glorious possessions.
Since atma vidy─Б can confer mokс╣гa ,
it follows that Lakс╣гm─л can confer mokс╣гa .)

Espa├▒ol

El gran sabio par─Б┼Ыara
quien recibi├│ el conocimiento sobre la verdad sobre la deidad suprema
De Boons otorgados por Vasiс╣гс╣нa y Pulastya
ha declarado

“T├║ eres, oh diosa,
el conocimiento sobre el alma,
El dador de mokс╣гa,
El objeto de logro “.

(El ┼Ъloka dice:

Eres el conocimiento sobre el yo o Atma Vidy─Б,

Lakс╣гm─л est├б en aposici├│n con Atma Vidy─Б.
El significado es que Atma Vidy─Б es una de sus vibh┼лtis o posesiones gloriosas.
Dado que Atma Vidy─Б puede conferir a Mokс╣гa,
Se deduce que Lakс╣гm─л puede conferir mokс╣гa.)

English

Koorathalvan too,
in elaboration of what is contained in the ┼Ыloka :-

“May Lakс╣гm─л confer happiness (on us) —
Lakс╣гm─л, looking at whose face, and with Her will as His aid,
the Lord creates, destroys and sustains all the worlds,
and grants also such things as svarga, naraka (hell) and mokс╣гa .
Since the two are engaged in the same work and
experience the same kind of delight,
the Lord cannot feel happy
if he performs the l─лl─Б of the work of the world
without her participation in it,”

Lakс╣гm─л, mirando a cuya cara, y con su voluntad como su ayuda,

experimentar el mismo tipo de deleite,
El Se├▒or no puede sentirse feliz

Sin su participaci├│n en ├йl "

English

Bhattar, also, has commented on the word Udaara (generous ) used in the ┼Ыruti (viz., ┼Ъr─л S┼лktam)
as an adjective for ┼Ъr─л in this manner:-

“How generous Thou art! O, Mother,
to the man who merely raises his hands folded in worship to Thee,
Thou grantest wealth, the enjoyment of his disembodied self and even paramapada
and yet Thou feelest ashamed that Thou hast not done anything adequate for him.”

Espa├▒ol

Bhattar, tambi├йn, ha comentado sobre la palabra Udaara (generoso) utilizado en el ┼Ъruti (a saber, ┼Ъr─л S┼лktam)
Como adjetivo para ┼Ъr─л de esta manera:-

“┬бQu├й generoso eres t├║, madre,
al hombre que simplemente levanta las manos dobladas en la adoraci├│n a ti,
T├║ otorga riqueza, el disfrute de su ser incorp├│reo e incluso paramapada
Y sin embargo, te sientes avergonzada
de que no hayas hecho nada adecuado para ├йl “.

(Critics who do not consider Lakс╣гm─л as an inseparable attribute or vi┼Ыeс╣гaс╣Зa of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa in the first part of Dvaya!)

Espa├▒ol

(Los cr├нticos
que no consideran a Lakс╣гm─л como un atributo inseparable o Vi┼Ыeс╣гaс╣Зa de N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa en la primera parte de Dvaya!)
Sostenes que las cosas como las cualidades del Salvador (compasi├│n, etc.) son atributos y no meros upalakс╣гaс╣Зa,
a pesar de que no pueden asumir la responsabilidad (bhara) de protecci├│n
y no puede tener la voluntad de proteger
(siendo solo las cualidades y, por lo tanto, no sonaciadas).

when this divine couple have the same pleasure or relish in all actions
and when they are both ┼Ыeс╣г─л s,
when there is the authority of the ┼Ы─Бstras for it?

In such vidy─Бs or forms of meditation as that of Pratardana,
although the Supreme Being is the object of knowledge,
we admit that sentient beings like Indra can be attributes of Bhagav─Бn just like non-sentient qualities.

Espa├▒ol

En tales vidy─Бs o formas de meditaci├│n como la de Pratardana,
Aunque el ser supremo es el objeto del conocimiento,
Admitimos que los seres sintientes como Indra
pueden ser atributos de Bhagav─Бn
al igual que las cualidades no sintientes.

Just as Bhagav─Бn with particular qualities (like omnipotence and compassion) and particular forms (vigraha)
indicated, respectively, by the words N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa and caraс╣Зau, (the two feet)
which are attributes of N─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa, forms a single up─Бya,
so also Bhagav─Бn with Lakс╣гm─л, who appears in the word ┼Ъr─лmat as an attribute in the eternal relationship of being His Spouse,
may without any impropriety, be considered as a single up─Бya.

Espa├▒ol

indicado, respectivamente, por las palabras n─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa y caraс╣Зau, (los dos pies)
que son atributos de n─Бr─Бyaс╣Зa, forma un solo up─Бya,
As├н tambi├йn Bhagav─Бn con Lakс╣гm─л, que aparece en la palabra ┼Ъr─лmat como un atributo
en la relaci├│n eterna de ser su c├│nyuge,
Puede que sin impropiedad, se considere como un solo up─Бya.

English

If it is said that we should give up all the attributes of the up─Бya in order to make the up─Бya single,
the dharma of being an up─Бya (i.e. up─Бyatva) will have to be given up also.

Espa├▒ol

Si se dice que deber├нamos renunciar a todos los atributos del up─Бya para hacer el up─Бya sencillo,
El dharma de ser un up─Бya (es decir, up─Бyatva) tambi├йn tendr├б que renunciar.

hence, though His supreme excellence is due to Thee,

A gem becomes valuable on account of its radiance.
It does not thereby become in itself worthless;
its value, which is natural to it, does not diminish thereby,
because its greatness is not due to anything else,”

рд╣рд╡рд┐рд░реН-рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖рдЩреНрдЧрд│рд┐рд▓реЗ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд╛-рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреБ-рдкреНрд░рднреГрддрд┐рдХрд│реБрдХреНрдХреБрдкреН рдкреЛрд▓реЗ

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

рдЙрднрдпреЛрд░реН рдЕрдкрд┐ +рдПрдХ-рд╢реЗрд╖рд┐рддреНрд╡рд╛рд╢реНрд░рдпрддреНрд╡рд╛рддреН
рд╣рд╡рд┐рд░реН-рд╡рд┐рд╢реЗрд╖реЗрд╖реБ рдЕрдЧреНрдирд╛-рд╡рд┐рд╖реНрдгреБ-рдкреНрд░рднреГрддреАрдирд╛рдореН рдЗрд╡
рдЖрддреНрдо-рд╕рдорд░реНрдкрдг-рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рд╕рдореНрдмрдиреНрдзрд┐-рднрд╛рд╡рд╕реНрдп рдирд╛рдиреБрдкрдкрдиреНрдирддреНрд╡рдореН ред

рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛рд╕-рдЯрд┐рдкреНрдкрдиреА

рдПрд╡рдВ рдирд┐рд╖реНрдХрд░реНрд╖рд┐рддреБрдВ рд╕рдорд░реНрдерд╕реНрдп рд╢рд┐рд╖реНрдпрд╕рдиреНрддрддрд┐рд░реН
рдЕрд░реНрд╡рд╛рдЪреАрди-рдХрд╛рд▓реЗ рдкреБрд░реЛрдбрд╛рд╢-рдпрдЬрди-рд╕реНрдерд╛рдиреЗ bread-рдкреБрд░реЛрдбрд╛рд╢-рд╡рд┐рдХреНрд░рдпрд╛рджрд┐-рд░рддрд╛
рдЗрддрд┐ рд╕реНрдореГрддрд┐рдкрдердореН рдЖрдпрд╛рддрд┐ рдХреЗрдирдЪрд┐рджреН рдЙрдХреНрддрдВ рд╣рд╛рд╕реНрдпрд╡рдЪрдирдореНред

English

In the case of certain special offerings (havis) enjoined in the Karmak─Бс╣Зс╕Нa,
the offering is made to two deities like Agni and Viс╣гс╣Зu as if they were single. So also in this offering of the soul called prapatti,
the two may, without any impropriety, be the single recipient.

Espa├▒ol

En el caso de ciertas ofrendas especiales (havis) ordenadas en el karmak─Бс╣Зс╕Нa,
La ofrenda se realiza a dos deidades como Agni y Viс╣гс╣Зu como si estuvieran solteras.
As├н tambi├йn en esta oferta del alma llamada Prapatti,
Los dos pueden, sin incorrecci├│n, ser el receptor ├║nico.

рдореВрд▓рдореН

рд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рддреНрд╡рд╛рджреАрдиреН рдХреГрддреНрд╡рд╛ рднрдЧрд╡рддрд┐ рдЧреБрдгрд╛рдиреН рдкреБрдВрд╕реНрддреНрд╡-рд╕реБ-рд▓рднрд╛рдиреН ред

рдХреНрд╖рдорд╛рджреАрдиреН рд╡рд╛ рднреЛрдХреНрддреБрдореН рднрд╡рддрд┐ рдпреБрд╡рдпреЛрд░реН рдЖрддреНрдордирд┐ рднрд┐рджрд╛ рее
(рд╢реНрд░реА-рдЧреБрдг-рд░рддреНрди-рдХреЛрд╢рдГ рейрек)

рдЗрддреНрдпреН-рдЙрдХреНрдд-рд░реАрддреНрдпрд╛

English

As stated in the ┼Ыloka,

“Youth and certain other qualities are common to Thee and Bhagav─Бn;
however you have divided other qualities between you for your enjoyment and (that in this way) :-
Bhagav─Бn has manly qualities like independence of others, control over enemies, firmness and the like
and Thou hast such feminine qualities as gentleness, existing only for the husband, compassion and forbearance”;

Espa├▒ol

Como se indica en el ┼Ъloka,

“Los j├│venes y ciertas otras cualidades son comunes para ti y Bhagav─Бn;
Sin embargo, ha dividido otras cualidades entre usted para su disfrute y (que de esta manera):-
Bhagav─Бn tiene cualidades varoniles como la independencia de los dem├бs, control sobre enemigos, firmeza y similares
y tienes cualidades femeninas como la gentileza, existente solo para el esposo, la compasi├│n y la tolerancia “;

тАШтАШрдпреБрд╡рддреНрд╡рд╛рджреМ рддреБрд▓реНрдпреЗрд╜рдкреНрдпрдкрд░рд╡рд╢рддрд╛ рд╢рддреНрд░реБрд╢рдордирд╕реНрдерд┐рд░рддреНрд╡рд╛рджреАрдиреН рдХреГрддреНрд╡рд╛ рднрдЧрд╡рддрд┐ рдЧреБрдгрд╛рдиреН рдкреБрдВрд╕реНрддреНрд╡рд╕реБрд▓рднрд╛рдиреН ред рддреНрд╡рдпрд┐ рд╕реНрддреНрд░реАрддреНрд╡реИрдХрд╛рдиреНрддрд╛рдиреНрдореГрджрд┐рдордкрддрд┐рдкрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдереНрдп рдХрд░реБрдгрд╛ рдХреНрд╖рдорд╛рджреАрдиреНрд╡рд╛ рднреЛрдХреНрддреБрдВ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рдпреБрд╡рдпреЛрд░рд╛рддреНрдордирд┐ рднрд┐рджрд╛тАЩтАЩ(рд╢реНрд░реА-рдЧреБрдг-рд░рддреНрди-рдХреЛрд╢рдГ рейрек) рдОрдйреНрдЧрд┐рд▒рдмрдбрд┐рдпреЗ

[[[резрепрез]]]

рдкрддреНрдиреНрдпрд╛ рдирд┐рддреНрдп-рдкрддрд┐-рдкрд╛рд░рд╛рд░реНрдереНрдпрд╛рджреН
рдпрд╛рдЧ-рддрдиреНрддреНрд░ рдЗрд╡ рдкрддрд┐-рдкреНрд░рд╛рдзрд╛рдиреНрдпреЗрди рд╢рд╛рд╕реНрддреНрд░реЗрд╖реБ +рдЙрдкрджреЗрд╢рд╛рдирд╛рдореН,

English

the wife is ever dependent on her Lord
and in the performance of yajnas or sacrifices, only the yajam─Бna is spoken of
(as his wife who participates in the performance is implicit, as it were,
in the word yajam─Бna,
even when one yajamana is referred to).

So also in regard to the teaching of the ┼Ы─Бstras,
the mention of a single person does not mean the absence of the wife who is, as it were, inseparable from her spouse.

Espa├▒ol

La esposa siempre depende de su Se├▒or
y en el desempe├▒o de Yajnas o sacrificios, solo se habla del Yajam─Бna
(Como su esposa que participa en la actuaci├│n est├б impl├нcita, por as├н decirlo,
En la palabra yajam─Бna,
incluso cuando se hace referencia a un Yajamana).

As├н tambi├йn con respecto a la ense├▒anza de los ┼Ъ─Бstras,
La menci├│n de una sola persona
no significa la ausencia de la esposa
que es, por as├н decirlo, inseparable de su c├│nyuge.

рдиреАрд▓рдореЗрдШрдГ (рд╕рдВ)

“рдкрдЩреНрдХрдЬрд╛рд▓рдпрд╛-рд╡рд▓реНрд▓рднрдореН рдПрдХрдореН рдПрд╡ рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпреА рдХрд░реЛрддрд┐ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдореНтАЭ

рдЗрддрд┐ рд╕реВрдХреНрддреЗрд░реН рдЕрдкреАрджрдореН рдПрд╡ рддрд╛рддреНрдкрд░реНрдпрдореН ред

English

In the verse :–

“Bhakti and prapatti are forms of knowledge which have, for their object, only Bhagav─Бn, the Lord of Lakс╣гm─л, who abides in the lotus
and (as) also the knowledge called the perfect enjoyment of Brahman has only Him for its object”

- in this verse this is really the meaning that Lakс╣гm─л, being included in Bhagav─Бn,
no separate mention is made of her.

Espa├▒ol

En el verso:-

“Bhakti y Prapatti son formas de conocimiento que tienen, por su objeto, solo Bhagav─Бn, el Se├▒or de Lakс╣гm─л, que permanece en el loto
y (como) tambi├йn el conocimiento llamado el disfrute perfecto de Brahman solo lo tiene por su objeto "

- En este verso, este es realmente el significado de que
Lakс╣гm─л, incluido en Bhagav─Бn,
No se hace una menci├│n separada de ella.

English

This may be seen also in the passage:

“Since Thou and Bhagav─Бn are thus inseparably united,

рди рджреЛрд╖рдГ ред

English

Those whose object is only mokс╣гa and who have no other aim, or interest, worship Lakс╣гm─л in her situation as laya (on the chest of Bhagav─Бn)
and as bhoga in the image of the spouse standing by the image of Bhagav─Бn.
But just as we bow before certain images of Bhagav─Бn (like Sant─Бnakс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa),
which bestow primarily the benefits desired in this world,
there is, for even mumukс╣гus, no impropriety in such actions as bowing before the image of Lakс╣гm─л installed in a separate shrine
and worshipped for certain worldly benefits (adhikaar─Бrch─Б),
just as we should bow before our mothers,
since in all images of Lakс╣гm─л (wherever they may be)
her being the Spouse of Viс╣гс╣Зu is an established fact.

Espa├▒ol

Aquellos cuyo objeto es solo mokс╣гa y que no tienen otro objetivo, ni inter├йs, adoran a Lakс╣гm─л en su situaci├│n como Laya (en el cofre de Bhagav─Бn)
y como bhoga en la imagen del c├│nyuge de pie junto a la imagen de Bhagav─Бn.
Pero tal como nos inclinamos antes de ciertas im├бgenes de Bhagav─Бn (como Sant─Бnakс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa),
que otorgan principalmente los beneficios deseados en este mundo,
Hay, incluso para Mumukс╣гus, no es incorrecci├│n en acciones como inclinarse ante la imagen de Lakс╣гm─л instalada en un santuario separado
y adorado por ciertos beneficios mundanos (adhikaar─Бrch─Б),
tal como deber├нamos inclinarnos ante nuestras madres,
Dado que en todas las im├бgenes de Lakс╣гm─л (donde sea que est├йn)

in the words of those who are disinterested,
those who are still so obstinate as not to give up their wrong notions,
